The factorial of <code>n</code> is the product of all positive integers less than or equal to <code>n</code>.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">factorial(n)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>n</code>: A non-negative integer. Type: Any integer type.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The factorial of <code>n</code>. Type: <a href="../data-types/int-uint">UInt64</a>.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT factorial(5)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─factorial(5)─┐
│          120 │
└──────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="width-bucket" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">width_bucket<a class="headerlink" href="#width-bucket" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Assigns a numeric value to a specific bucket within a defined range, dividing the range into equal-width intervals.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">widthBucket(operand, low, high, count)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Alias: <code>WIDTH_BUCKET</code></p><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>operand</code>: The value to be placed into a bucket. Type: Any numeric type.</li><li><code>low</code>: The lower bound of the range. Type: Any numeric type.</li><li><code>high</code>: The upper bound of the range. Type: Any numeric type.</li><li><code>count</code>: The number of equal-width buckets. Type: <a href="../data-types/int-uint">UInt*</a> (must be non-zero).</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The bucket number (1 to <code>count</code>), <code>0</code> if <code>operand &lt; low</code>, or <code>count + 1</code> if <code>operand &gt;= high</code>. Type: <a href="../data-types/int-uint">UInt64</a>.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT widthBucket(5.5, 0, 10, 2)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─widthBucket(5.5, 0, 10, 2)─┐
│                          2 │
└────────────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="proportionsztest" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">proportionsZTest<a class="headerlink" href="#proportionsztest" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Performs a two-proportion Z-test to compare the proportions of successes from two independent populations. It returns statistical metrics including the Z-statistic, p-value, and confidence interval.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">proportionsZTest(successes_x, successes_y, trials_x, trials_y, conf_level, pool_type)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>successes_x</code>: Number of successes in population <code>x</code>. Type: <a href="../data-types/int-uint">UInt64</a>.</li><li><code>successes_y</code>: Number of successes in population <code>y</code>. Type: <a href="../data-types/int-uint">UInt64</a>.</li><li><code>trials_x</code>: Total number of trials in population <code>x</code>. Type: <a href="../data-types/int-uint">UInt64</a>.</li><li><code>trials_y</code>: Total number of trials in population <code>y</code>. Type: <a href="../data-types/int-uint">UInt64</a>.</li><li><code>conf_level</code>: The desired confidence level for the test (e.g., 0.95 for 95%). Type: <a href="../data-types/float">Float64</a>.</li><li><code>pool_type</code>: Specifies whether to use a &#x27;pooled&#x27; or &#x27;unpooled&#x27; estimate for the standard error. Type: <a href="../data-types/string">String</a>.</li></ul><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>For argument <code>pool_type</code>: In the pooled version, the two proportions are averaged, and only one proportion is used to estimate the standard error. In the unpooled version, the two proportions are used separately.</p></div></div><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>A tuple containing:</p><ul><li><code>z_stat</code>: The calculated Z-statistic. Type: <a href="../data-types/float">Float64</a>.</li><li><code>p_val</code>: The p-value of the test. Type: <a href="../data-types/float">Float64</a>.</li><li><code>ci_low</code>: The lower bound of the confidence interval. Type: <a href="../data-types/float">Float64</a>.</li><li><code>ci_high</code>: The upper bound of the confidence interval. Type: <a href="../data-types/float">Float64</a>.</li></ul><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT proportionsZTest(10, 11, 100, 101, 0.95, &#x27;unpooled&#x27;)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─proportionsZTest(10, 11, 100, 101, 0.95, &#x27;unpooled&#x27;)───────────────────────────────┐
│ (-0.20656724435948853,0.8363478437079654,-0.09345975390115283,0.07563797172293502) │
└────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></article><div class="flex items-center justify-end h-10" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="italic text-caption"><span>Updated<!-- --> Math Functions reference\nmeta:\n    description: Functions for mathematical operations.\nheadingMaxLevels: 2\n---\n\n# Mathematical functions\n\nThe following functions perform mathematical operations.\n\n## e\n\nReturns the mathematical constant `e`, also known as Euler's number.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\ne()\n```\n\n### Returns\n\nThe value of `e`. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT e()\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─e()────────────────┐\n│ 2.718281828459045  │\n└────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## pi\n\nReturns the mathematical constant `π` (Pi).\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\npi()\n```\n\n### Returns\n\nThe value of `π`. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT pi()\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─pi()───────────────┐\n│ 3.141592653589793  │\n└────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## exp\n\nCalculates the exponential function, raising `e` to the power of the given argument.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nexp(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The exponent. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe result of `e^x`. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT round(exp(-1), 4)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─round(exp(-1), 4)─┐\n│            0.3679 │\n└───────────────────┘\n```\n\n## log\n\nComputes the natural logarithm (base `e`) of a number.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nlog(x)\n```\n\nAlias: `ln(x)`\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The number for which to calculate the natural logarithm. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe natural logarithm of `x`. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT log(10)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─log(10)────────────┐\n│ 2.302585092994046  │\n└────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## exp2\n\nCalculates 2 raised to the power of the given argument.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nexp2(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The exponent. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe result of `2^x`. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT exp2(3)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─exp2(3)─┐\n│       8 │\n└─────────┘\n```\n\n## intExp2\n\nCalculates 2 raised to the power of the given argument, returning the result as an unsigned 64-bit integer.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nintExp2(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The exponent. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe result of `2^x`. Type: [UInt64](../data-types/int-uint).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT intExp2(5)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─intExp2(5)─┐\n│         32 │\n└────────────┘\n```\n\n## log2\n\nComputes the binary logarithm (base 2) of a number.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nlog2(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The number for which to calculate the binary logarithm. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe base 2 logarithm of `x`. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT log2(8)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─log2(8)─┐\n│       3 │\n└─────────┘\n```\n\n## exp10\n\nCalculates 10 raised to the power of the given argument.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nexp10(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The exponent. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe result of `10^x`. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT exp10(2)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─exp10(2)─┐\n│      100 │\n└──────────┘\n```\n\n## intExp10\n\nCalculates 10 raised to the power of the given argument, returning the result as an unsigned 64-bit integer.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nintExp10(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The exponent. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe result of `10^x`. Type: [UInt64](../data-types/int-uint).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT intExp10(3)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─intExp10(3)─┐\n│        1000 │\n└─────────────┘\n```\n\n## log10\n\nComputes the common logarithm (base 10) of a number.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nlog10(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The number for which to calculate the common logarithm. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe base 10 logarithm of `x`. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT log10(100)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─log10(100)─┐\n│          2 │\n└────────────┘\n```\n\n## sqrt\n\nCalculates the square root of a non-negative number.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nsqrt(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The number for which to calculate the square root. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe square root of `x`. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT sqrt(25)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─sqrt(25)─┐\n│        5 │\n└──────────┘\n```\n\n## cbrt\n\nCalculates the cube root of a number.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\ncbrt(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The number for which to calculate the cube root. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe cube root of `x`. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT cbrt(27)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─cbrt(27)─┐\n│        3 │\n└──────────┘\n```\n\n## erf\n\nComputes the error function of a given value. This function is often used in probability and statistics.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nerf(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The input value. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe error function of `x`. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT erf(3 / sqrt(2))\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─erf(divide(3, sqrt(2)))─┐\n│      0.9973002039367398 │\n└─────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## erfc\n\nComputes the complementary error function, which is `1 - erf(x)`. This function provides higher precision for large `x` values compared to directly calculating `1 - erf(x)`.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nerfc(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The input value. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe complementary error function of `x`. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT erfc(0)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─erfc(0)─┐\n│       1 │\n└─────────┘\n```\n\n## lgamma\n\nCalculates the natural logarithm of the absolute value of the gamma function.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nlgamma(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The input value. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe natural logarithm of the gamma function of `x`. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT lgamma(5)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─lgamma(5)──────────┐\n│ 3.1780538303479453 │\n└────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## tgamma\n\nCalculates the gamma function of a given value.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\ngamma(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The input value. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe gamma function of `x`. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT gamma(5)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─gamma(5)─┐\n│       24 │\n└──────────┘\n```\n\n## sin\n\nComputes the sine of an angle given in radians.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nsin(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The angle in radians. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe sine of `x`. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT sin(pi() / 2)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─sin(divide(pi(), 2))─┐\n│                    1 │\n└──────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## cos\n\nComputes the cosine of an angle given in radians.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\ncos(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The angle in radians. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe cosine of `x`. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT cos(pi())\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─cos(pi())─┐\n│        -1 │\n└───────────┘\n```\n\n## tan\n\nComputes the tangent of an angle given in radians.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\ntan(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The angle in radians. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe tangent of `x`. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT tan(pi() / 4)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─tan(divide(pi(), 4))─┐\n│                    1 │\n└──────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## asin\n\nComputes the arc sine (inverse sine) of a value, returning the angle in radians.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nasin(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The value for which to calculate the arc sine (must be between -1 and 1). Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe arc sine of `x` in radians. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT asin(1)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─asin(1)────────────┐\n│ 1.5707963267948966 │\n└────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## acos\n\nComputes the arc cosine (inverse cosine) of a value, returning the angle in radians.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nacos(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The value for which to calculate the arc cosine (must be between -1 and 1). Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe arc cosine of `x` in radians. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT acos(0)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─acos(0)────────────┐\n│ 1.5707963267948966 │\n└────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## atan\n\nComputes the arc tangent (inverse tangent) of a value, returning the angle in radians.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\natan(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The value for which to calculate the arc tangent. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe arc tangent of `x` in radians. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT atan(1)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─atan(1)────────────┐\n│ 0.7853981633974483 │\n└────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## pow\n\nCalculates the result of raising a base number to a specified exponent.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\npow(x, y)\n```\n\nAlias: `power(x, y)`\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The base number. Type: [(U)Int8/16/32/64](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n- `y`: The exponent. Type: [(U)Int8/16/32/64](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe value of `x` raised to the power of `y`. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT pow(2, 4)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─pow(2, 4)─┐\n│        16 │\n└───────────┘\n```\n\n## cosh\n\nComputes the hyperbolic cosine of an angle.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\ncosh(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The angle, in radians. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe hyperbolic cosine of `x`. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT cosh(0)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─cosh(0)──┐\n│        1 │\n└──────────┘\n```\n\n## acosh\n\nComputes the inverse hyperbolic cosine of a value.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nacosh(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The value for which to calculate the inverse hyperbolic cosine (must be `\u003e= 1`). Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe inverse hyperbolic cosine of `x` in radians. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT acosh(1)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─acosh(1)─┐\n│        0 │\n└──────────┘\n```\n\n## sinh\n\nComputes the hyperbolic sine of an angle.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nsinh(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The angle, in radians. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe hyperbolic sine of `x`. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT sinh(0)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─sinh(0)──┐\n│        0 │\n└──────────┘\n```\n\n## asinh\n\nComputes the inverse hyperbolic sine of a value.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nasinh(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The value for which to calculate the inverse hyperbolic sine. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe inverse hyperbolic sine of `x` in radians. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT asinh(0)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─asinh(0)─┐\n│        0 │\n└──────────┘\n```\n\n## tanh\n\nComputes the hyperbolic tangent of an angle.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\ntanh(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The angle, in radians. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe hyperbolic tangent of `x`. Type: [Float*](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT tanh(0)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─tanh(0)─┐\n│       0 │\n└─────────┘\n```\n\n## atanh\n\nComputes the inverse hyperbolic tangent of a value.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\natanh(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The value for which to calculate the inverse hyperbolic tangent (must be between -1 and 1, exclusive). Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe inverse hyperbolic tangent of `x` in radians. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT atanh(0)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─atanh(0)─┐\n│        0 │\n└──────────┘\n```\n\n## atan2\n\nCalculates the angle in radians between the positive x-axis and a point `(x, y)` in the Euclidean plane. This function correctly handles all four quadrants.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\natan2(y, x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `y`: The y-coordinate of the point. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n- `x`: The x-coordinate of the point. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe angle `θ` in radians, where `-π \u003c θ \u003c= π`. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT atan2(1, 1)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌────────atan2(1, 1)─┐\n│ 0.7853981633974483 │\n└────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## hypot\n\nCalculates the length of the hypotenuse of a right-angled triangle given the lengths of its two shorter sides. This function is designed to avoid overflow or underflow issues with very large or small inputs.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nhypot(x, y)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The length of the first side (cathetus). Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n- `y`: The length of the second side (cathetus). Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe length of the hypotenuse. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT hypot(3, 4)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─hypot(3, 4)─┐\n│           5 │\n└─────────────┘\n```\n\n## log1p\n\nComputes the natural logarithm of `1 + x`. This function offers improved precision for `x` values close to zero compared to `log(1 + x)`.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nlog1p(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The input value (must be `\u003e -1`). Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe natural logarithm of `1 + x`. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT log1p(0)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─log1p(0)─┐\n│        0 │\n└──────────┘\n```\n\n## sign\n\nDetermines the sign of a numeric value.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nsign(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: Any numeric value. Type: All numeric types.\n\n### Returns\n\n- `-1` if `x \u003c 0`\n- `0` if `x = 0`\n- `1` if `x \u003e 0`\n\nType: [Int8](../data-types/int-uint).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT sign(-5)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─sign(-5)─┐\n│       -1 │\n└──────────┘\n```\n\n## sigmoid\n\nApplies the sigmoid activation function, which maps any real-valued number to a value between 0 and 1. This is commonly used in machine learning.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nsigmoid(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The input value. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe sigmoid of `x`. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT round(sigmoid(0), 5)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─round(sigmoid(0), 5)─┐\n│                  0.5 │\n└──────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## degrees\n\nConverts an angle from radians to degrees.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\ndegrees(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The angle in radians. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe angle in degrees. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT degrees(pi())\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─degrees(pi())─┐\n│           180 │\n└───────────────┘\n```\n\n## radians\n\nConverts an angle from degrees to radians.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nradians(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The angle in degrees. Type: [(U)Int*](../data-types/int-uint), [Float*](../data-types/float) or [Decimal*](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe angle in radians. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT radians(90)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─radians(90)────────┐\n│ 1.5707963267948966 │\n└────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## factorial\n\nComputes the factorial of a non-negative integer. The factorial of `n` is the product of all positive integers less than or equal to `n`.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nfactorial(n)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `n`: A non-negative integer. Type: Any integer type.\n\n### Returns\n\nThe factorial of `n`. Type: [UInt64](../data-types/int-uint).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT factorial(5)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─factorial(5)─┐\n│          120 │\n└──────────────┘\n```\n\n## width_bucket\n\nAssigns a numeric value to a specific bucket within a defined range, dividing the range into equal-width intervals.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nwidthBucket(operand, low, high, count)\n```\n\nAlias: `WIDTH_BUCKET`\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `operand`: The value to be placed into a bucket. Type: Any numeric type.\n- `low`: The lower bound of the range. Type: Any numeric type.\n- `high`: The upper bound of the range. Type: Any numeric type.\n- `count`: The number of equal-width buckets. Type: [UInt*](../data-types/int-uint) (must be non-zero).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe bucket number (1 to `count`), `0` if `operand \u003c low`, or `count + 1` if `operand \u003e= high`. Type: [UInt64](../data-types/int-uint).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT widthBucket(5.5, 0, 10, 2)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─widthBucket(5.5, 0, 10, 2)─┐\n│                          2 │\n└────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## proportionsZTest\n\nPerforms a two-proportion Z-test to compare the proportions of successes from two independent populations. It returns statistical metrics including the Z-statistic, p-value, and confidence interval.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nproportionsZTest(successes_x, successes_y, trials_x, trials_y, conf_level, pool_type)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `successes_x`: Number of successes in population `x`. Type: [UInt64](../data-types/int-uint).\n- `successes_y`: Number of successes in population `y`. Type: [UInt64](../data-types/int-uint).\n- `trials_x`: Total number of trials in population `x`. Type: [UInt64](../data-types/int-uint).\n- `trials_y`: Total number of trials in population `y`. Type: [UInt64](../data-types/int-uint).\n- `conf_level`: The desired confidence level for the test (e.g., 0.95 for 95%). Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n- `pool_type`: Specifies whether to use a 'pooled' or 'unpooled' estimate for the standard error. Type: [String](../data-types/string).\n\n{% callout type=\"info\" %}\nFor argument `pool_type`: In the pooled version, the two proportions are averaged, and only one proportion is used to estimate the standard error. In the unpooled version, the two proportions are used separately.\n{% /callout %}\n\n### Returns\n\nA tuple containing:\n- `z_stat`: The calculated Z-statistic. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n- `p_val`: The p-value of the test. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n- `ci_low`: The lower bound of the confidence interval. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n- `ci_high`: The upper bound of the confidence interval. Type: [Float64](../data-types/float).\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT proportionsZTest(10, 11, 100, 101, 0.95, 'unpooled')\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─proportionsZTest(10, 11, 100, 101, 0.95, 'unpooled')───────────────────────────────┐\n│ (-0.20656724435948853,0.8363478437079654,-0.09345975390115283,0.07563797172293502) │\n└────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"8:[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"className\":\"relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 xl:grid xl:grid-cols-[1fr_280px]\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"className\":\"max-w-4xl text-body md:px-4 md:pb-20 relative\",\"role\":\"main\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L20\",null,{\"pageContent\":\"$21\",\"pagePath\":\"app/__sql-reference/functions/math-functions\",\"children\":[\"$\",\"article\",null,{\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L22\",null,{\"level\":1,\"name\":\"Heading\",\"children\":\"Mathematical functions\"}],[\"$\",\"p\",null,{\"children\":\"The following functions perform mathematical operations.\"}],[\"$\",\"$L22\",null,{\"level\":2,\"name\":\"Heading\",\"children\":\"e\"}],[\"$\",\"p\",null,{\"children\":[\"Returns the mathematical constant \",[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"e\"}],\", also known as Euler's number.\"]}],[\"$\",\"$L22\",null,{\"level\":3,\"name\":\"Heading\",\"children\":\"Syntax\"}],\"$L23\",[\"$\",\"$L22\",null,{\"level\":3,\"name\":\"Heading\",\"children\":\"Returns\"}],[\"$\",\"p\",null,{\"children\":[\"The value of \",[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"e\"}],\".
